<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">■</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">4.1 出力形式</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>

<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >本システムから出力される電子ファイルは、利用目的に応じて以下の3つの型に分類される。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >利用目的に応じて以下の3つの型に分類される。各帳票の機能要件に基づき、適切な形式を定義する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >・</td>
<td >PDF出力型： 閲覧・保管・印刷を目的とした原本形式で出力。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >・</td>
<td >データ出力型（CSV/Excel）： 加工・分析・他システム連携を目的としたデータ形式で出力。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >・</td>
<td >帳票形式型： 原本形式から軽微な修正を加えて再配布することを目的としてExcel形式で出力。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" style="background-color:#F2F2F2;color:#F2F2F2">業務シーン</td>
<td colspan="26" style="background-color:#F2F2F2;color:#F2F2F2">内容</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >伝票登録</td>
<td colspan="26" >登録した内容について伝票（単票や一覧表）形式で出力し、決裁を取る。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >監査・検査対応</td>
<td colspan="26" >集計表や監査資料をPDF出力し、会計検査や監査委員による監査で提出する。あるいは準備資料として使用する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >予算・決算対応</td>
<td colspan="26" >完成した予算書、決算書をPDF出力し、議会に提出する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >→証跡を残す、当時の記録として改ざんを防止する、責任の所在を明らかにするためにPDF出力する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td colspan="5" style="background-color:#F2F2F2;color:#F2F2F2">業務シーン</td>
<td colspan="26" style="background-color:#F2F2F2;color:#F2F2F2">内容</td>

<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >予算編成準備</td>
<td colspan="26" >新年度の科目体系を検討する際、現行マスタをデータ出力して判断する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >監査・検査対応</td>
<td colspan="26" >会計検査や監査委員による監査準備過程で、データの不備や誤りがあった場合にデータ出力し、分析する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >マスタ一括更新</td>
<td colspan="26" >現行データを一度出力し、修正したものを一括インポート（アップロード）する際の下書きとして利用する。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >外部連携</td>

<td >日付</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >あり</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >システム間連携やExcelでの日付認識を確実にするため&quot;&quot;で囲む。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >金額</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >決定金額、予算額</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >-</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >999999999999</td>
<td >数値</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >なし</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >二次加工（再計算）を優先し、カンマは出力しない。囲みも行わない。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >-</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td colspan="5" >あああ</td>
<td >文字列</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >あり</td>
